When a model signs with you, look at it from her perspective. She's taking a risk. She's giving up her income. At the end of the day, she doesn't know if you're legit. [3:47:13](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wVpPHmqYkNA&t=13633s) so many agencies nowadays making overpromises and massively underd delivering, your job in the first seven days will dictate whether she thinks of you as another agency that she made a bad decision with or the final and right move that she has made. [3:47:43](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wVpPHmqYkNA&t=13663s) posts a random reel that you recommended her and gets 500 views. She's confused. She's doing the same thing she was. [5:03:00](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wVpPHmqYkNA&t=18180s) repurposing, follow andf follow, cubid AI, nude, and flash reels. Now, why do I include nude and flash reels?
